***kleven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleven</a> (21308)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clēven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">clivon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klibāną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gleybʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stick, to be attached glue-like
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ineens.html>Ineens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:merkte.html>merkte</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kauwgom.html>kauwgom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:sandaal.html>sandaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleefde.html>kleefde</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Suddenly she noticed that there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> chewing gum <b>sticking</b> to her sandal.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to glue, to adhere something on/to something else, to stick to/on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>Zij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plaagt.html>plaagt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vader.html>vader</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> kauwgum <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:snor.html>snor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleven</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">She <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> teasing her dad by <b>sticking</b> chewing gum on his moustache.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be sticky
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:deze.html>Deze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grondstof.html>grondstof</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:kleeft.html>kleeft</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:heel.html>heel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">This resource <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> very very <b>sticky</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bumperkleven.html>bumperkleven</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kleverig.html>kleverig</a> (26173)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kleven.html>kleven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stick</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-erig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***klier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klier.html>klier</a> (15660)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cliere</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sco">clyre</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tumour</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klier.html>klier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klieren.html>klieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kliertje.html>kliertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>gland</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">gland</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">secretory structure</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> someone suffering from a skin disease or glandular swelling</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klier.html>klier</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klieren.html>klieren</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kliertje.html>kliertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>an obnoxious person</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clicken</i>, of imitative origin.

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsoletel<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to knock, to make a knocking sound</li></ol>

***kliko.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kliko.html>kliko</a> (116078)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <a href = vnd.unilang:kliko.html>Kliko</a>, acronym of proper names Klinkenberg and <a href = vnd.unilang:koster.html>Koster</a>, a company that historically <a href = vnd.unilang:sold.html>sold</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wheelie.html>wheelie</a> bins.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kliko.html>kliko</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kliko.html>kliko</a>'s</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:wheelie.html>wheelie</a> bin (outdoor tall plastic garbage container with two <a href = vnd.unilang:wheels.html>wheels</a> to one side)</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">minicontainer</span></li>

***kliniek.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kliniek.html>kliniek</a> (3674)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:clinique.html>clinique</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la"><a href = vnd.unilang:clinicus.html>clinicus</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a bed-ridden person, one baptized on a sick-bed, a physician</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλινικός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klinikós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pertaining to a <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλίνη</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klínē</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">κλίνειν</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klínein</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lean, incline</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kliniek.html>kliniek</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klinieken.html>klinieken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kliniek.html>kliniekje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A clinic, type of hospital</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klinkend.html>klinkend</a> (104304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:klinkend.html>klinkend</a></b>

***klip.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klip.html>klip</a> (31134)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clippe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klippa</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klippō</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klip.html>klip</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klippen.html>klippen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klip.html>klipje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>rock or <a href = vnd.unilang:cliff.html>cliff</a> in or around sea water
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klif.html>klif</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">dune</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:sandy.html>sandy</a> hill</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rock on <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a>, e.g. used as a habitat by animals</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">boulder</span>, piece of rock</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

</p>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cloec</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*cluoc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klōkaz</i>.

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***klok.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klok.html>klok</a> (2443)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clocke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klokka</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Irish" class="extiw" title="w:Old Irish">Old Irish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sga">clocc</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Celtic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Celtic language">Proto-Celtic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="cel-pro">*klokkos</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately of onomatopoeic origin.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klokhuis.html>klokhuis</a> (82131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clochuus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bell tower</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klok.html>klok</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house, casing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***klokken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klokken.html>klokken</a> (6966)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clocke</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokken.html>klokken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klok.html>klok</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokken.html>klokken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to time, clock</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Onomatopoeic. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">glug</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cluck</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokken.html>klokken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of water</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gurgle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">of chickens and other fowl</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cluck</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection_2">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klok.html>klok</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_3">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klokken.html>klokken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to clock, to measure duration (of)</li></ol>

***klomp.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klomp.html>klomp</a> (25298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clompe</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump or mass of metal, wooden shoe, clump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klumpo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klumpô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump, clump, mass; clasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*glembʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clamp, mass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs">klumpa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clump</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:klump.html>Klump</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Klumpen</i>. Related to <span class="Latn" lang="en">clamp</span>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:252px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg/250px-SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg" decoding="async" width="250" height="199" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg/375px-SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fa/SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg/500px-SouvenirKlompjes1212.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1914" data-file-height="1522" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div><i><a href = vnd.unilang:souvenir.html>Souvenir</a><b><a href = vnd.unilang:klompjes.html>klompjes</a></b></i><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:souvenir.html>Souvenir</a> <b>clogs</b></div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klomp.html>klomp</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klompen.html>klompen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klompje.html>klompje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A wooden shoe, clog.</li>
<li>A mass, a nugget, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">lump</span>, a <span class="Latn" lang="en">chunk</span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:klomp.html>klomp</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>

***klooien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klooien.html>klooien</a> (11147)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clôyen</i> (variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clouwen</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*clōien</i>  (variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*clouen</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klawjaną</i>; possibly related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klooi.html>klooi</a></i> and a doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klauwen.html>klauwen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>To (give a) beat(ing)</li>
<li>To mess around</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To sleep with, i.e. share the <a href = vnd.unilang:bed.html>bed</a>, with; to fuck</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clôot</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klōt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klautaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cleat</i>. Related to Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluit.html>kluit</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump; lump of earth</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klont.html>klont</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***klopje.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klopje.html>klopje</a> (38119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Uncertain, perhaps in reference to Christ who knocked (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:kloppen.html>kloppen</a></i>) at the <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> of a woman's heart.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klopje.html>klopje</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klopje.html>klopjes</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unmarried woman who <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> dedicated her life to service to the Church.</li></ol>

***kloppen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kloppen.html>kloppen</a> (2495)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cloppen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*cloppōn</i>, probably onomatopoeic. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">klopfen</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kloppen.html>kloppen</a></i>.

***klos.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klos.html>klos</a> (10407)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">closse</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klos.html>klos</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klos.html>klossen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klosje.html>klosje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:spool.html>spool</a>, bobbin</li>
<li>wooden or metal reel or similar object</li>
<li>hardwood beam for sewing into planks, notably oak</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> testicle</li>
<li>klutz, clumsy person</li>
<li>target, victim (of a problem or joke)</li>
<li>lump, clod</li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:cocoon.html>cocoon</a>,<a href = vnd.unilang:chrysalis.html>chrysalis</a></li>
<li>corn cob</li>
<li>fir-cone</li>
<li>horse's (lower) <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a>; protuberance thereupon</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

***klucht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a> (23790)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cluft</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">clucht</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kluft</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kluftiz</i> (whence also German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kluft</i>, English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cleft</i>). The word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klieven.html>klieven</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to <a href = vnd.unilang:cleave.html>cleave</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and the Middle Dutch meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> at first "separation, department", <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> also "neighbourhood of a town". The sense shifted to its modern meaning only in early modern Dutch times, starting with "nonsense, prattle" and then "joke, humorous story".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluchten.html>kluchten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>kluchtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:theater.html>theater</a> play, farce</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">esp. Brabantian, figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> chaotic, loud and/or ridiculous situation
<dl><dd><i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeg.html>zeg</a>, 'k <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vlug.html>vlug</a> afgetrapt!"</i></dd>
<dd>'<i>Twas such a mess <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> there, I left as soon as I could!</i></dd>
<dd><i>"Da's <a href = vnd.unilang:geen.html>geen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bedrijf.html>bedrijf</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b>!"</i></dd>
<dd><i>That company <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sooo mismanaged, hilarious!</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:letterkunde.html>letterkunde</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:meestal.html>meestal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kort.html>kort</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toneelstuk.html>toneelstuk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waarvan.html>waarvan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> plot <a href = vnd.unilang:komisch.html>komisch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i>"<a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koe.html>koe</a>" <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschreven.html>geschreven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> Bredero.</i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:lachwekkend.html>lachwekkend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voorval.html>voorval</a>
<dl><dd><ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:mannen.html>Mannen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hadden.html>hadden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wij.html>wij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> Sinterklaas-avond <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:pret.html>pret</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:klucht.html>klucht</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:om.html>om</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bang.html>bang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijne.html>mijne</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jongens.html>jongens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:ha.html>ha</a>!<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup></i> </li></ul></dd></dl></li>
<li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(pejoratief)</span> schijnvertoning, schertsvertoning

***kluis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kluis.html>kluis</a> (1785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cluse</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clūsa</i>, variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">clausa</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluis.html>kluis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluizen.html>kluizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluisje.html>kluisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A safe.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">in the diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A cashbox.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">often diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A locker.</li>
<li>A hermit's cell.</li>
<li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:hermitage.html>hermitage</a>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">safe</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:brandkast.html>brandkast</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">locker</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">locker</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">hermit's cell</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:cel.html>cel</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:hermitage.html>hermitage</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hermitage.html>hermitage</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kluizenarij</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluisteren.html>kluister</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a fetter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">claudō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">close, shut</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To fetter, hog-tie or (rather) restrain in remaining movement</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figurative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To bind, restrict, as by a spell, fascination etc.</li></ol>

***kluiven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kluiven.html>kluiven</a> (74929)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cluven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*klūvon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klūbōną</i>. Originally a weak verb, it became strong by analogy with other verbs.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluiven.html>kluiven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to gnaw, to nibble</li>
<li>to bite (a piece of meat) into <a href = vnd.unilang:smaller.html>smaller</a> chunks</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kluns.html>kluns</a> (14630)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluns.html>Kluns</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluns.html>kluns</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klunzen.html>klunzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kluns.html>klunsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>clumsy person, klutz</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cluwen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kliuwīn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kliuwīną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*klewô</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*glew-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clew</i>.
</p>
